Universe, creation|Heelal, die skepping
Use this domain for general words referring to the physical universe. Some languages may not have a single word for the universe and may have to use a phrase such as 'rain, soil, and things of the sky' or 'sky, land, and water' or a descriptive phrase such as 'everything you can see' or 'everything that exists'.|Gebruik hierdie domein vir algemene woorde wat verwys na die fisiese heelal. Sommige tale kan nie &#39;n enkele woord vir die heelal en mag het om &#39;n frase soos &quot;reën, grond, en dinge van die hemel&quot; of &quot;lug, grond, water en &#39;n beskrywende of frase soos&quot; alles wat jy kan gebruik sien &quot;of&quot; alles wat bestaan.
(1) What words refer to everything we can see?|(1) Watter woorde verwys na alles wat ons kan sien nie?
universe, creation, cosmos, heaven and earth, macrocosm, everything that exists|heelal, die skepping, die kosmos, die hemel en die aarde, makrokosmos, alles wat bestaan
Sky|Sky
Use this domain for words related to the sky.|Gebruik hierdie domein woorde in verband met die lug.
(1) What words are used to refer to the sky?|(1) Watter woorde gebruik om te verwys na die hemel?
sky, firmament, canopy, vault|lug, uitspansel, sondak, kluis
(2) What words refer to the air around the earth?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na die lug rondom die aarde?
air, atmosphere, airspace, stratosphere, ozone layer|lug, atmosfeer, lugruim, stratosfeer, osoonlaag
(3) What words are used to refer to the place or area beyond the sky?|(3) Watter woorde gebruik om te verwys na die plek of gebied buite die hemel?
heaven, space, outer space, ether, void, solar system|hemel, ruimte, die buitenste ruimte, eter, nietig, sonnestelsel
(4) What words describe something in the sky or something that happens in the sky?|(4) Watter woorde iets in die lug of iets wat gebeur in die lug te beskryf?
aerial, heavenly, atmospheric, stratospheric, celestial,|lug, hemelse, atmosferiese, stratosfeer, hemelse,
(5) What words describe the appearance of the sky?|(5) Watter woorde beskryf die voorkoms van die lug?
blue, clear, black (night), cloudy, cloud filled, brilliant, dark, night sky, foreboding, stormy, dark, star studded|blou, helder, swart (nag), bewolk, wolk, briljante, donker, nag lug, onheilspellend, stormagtige, donker, sterbelaaide
(6) What words refer to the edge of the sky where it meets the ground?|(6) Watter woorde verwys na die rand van die lug waar dit aan die grond?
horizon, skyline|horison, skyline
(7) What words refer to something in the sky?|(7) Wat woorde verwys na iets in die lug?
heavenly body, celestial body, luminary|hemelse liggaam hemelliggaam, uitblinker
(8) What words refer to the lights that appear in the northern (or southern) sky?|(8) Watter woorde verwys na die ligte wat in die noordelike (of suidelike) lug verskyn?
aurora borealis, northern lights|aurora borealis, noordelike ligte
(9) What words refer to something being in the sky?|(9) Watter woorde verwys na iets wat in die hemel?
aloft, up in the sky, up in the air,|omhoog, tot in die hemel, in die lug,
Sun|Sun
Use this domain for words related to the sun. The sun does three basic things. It moves, it gives light, and it gives heat. These three actions are involved in the meanings of most of the words in this domain. Since the sun moves below the horizon, many words refer to it setting or rising. Since the sun is above the clouds, many words refer to it moving behind the clouds and the clouds blocking its light. The sun's light and heat also produce secondary effects. The sun causes plants to grow, and it causes damage to things.|Gebruik hierdie domein woorde in verband met die son. Die son doen drie basiese dinge. Dit beweeg, dit gee lig, en dit gee hitte. Hierdie drie aksies betrokke in die betekenis van die meeste van die woorde in hierdie gebied. Sedert die son beweeg onder die horison, baie woorde verwys na dit opstel of styg. Sedert die son bo die wolke, baie woorde verwys na dit beweeg agter die wolke en die wolke in die lig daarvan blokkeer. Lig en die son se hitte te produseer ook sekondêre effekte. Die son veroorsaak plante om te groei, en dit skade aan dinge veroorsaak.
(1) What words refer to the sun?|(1) Watter woorde verwys na die son?
sun, solar, sol, daystar, our star|son, son, sol, Daystar, ons ster
(2) What words refer to how the sun moves?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
rise, set, cross the sky, come up, go down, sink|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(3) What words refer to the time when the sun rises?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
dawn, sunrise, sunup, daybreak, cockcrow,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(4) What words refer to the time when the sun is at its highest point?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
noon, zenith,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(5) What words refer to the time when the sun sets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunset, dusk, sundown, twilight, eventide,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(6) What words refer to when the sun is shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
shine, sunny, bright, give light, be sunshiny, daytime,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(7) What words refer to the sun shining through the clouds?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
come out, break through (the clouds), go behind (a cloud)|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(8) What words describe where the sun is shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunlit, be (out) in the sun, lit by the sun, shine on, be in the sunlight, sunny (spot)|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(9) What words describe when or where the sun doesn't shine?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
shade, eclipse of the sun, sunless, shady, shadow, eclipse (v),|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(10) What words refer to the light of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunlight, ray, sunshine, beam, light, sunbeam, radiance, glow, sparkle, glisten, glare|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(11) What words describe the brightness of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
bright, intense, brilliant, blinding, glaring, glistening, luminous, dim|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(12) What refer to the sun heating things?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
warm, heat, dry|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(13) What else does the sun do?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
looks down on|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(14) What words describe the damage done by sunlight?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunburn, sunstroke, suntan, tan, heatstroke, heat prostration, sun damage, fading from the sun, bleached by the sun|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(15) What do people use to protect themselves from the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunglasses, shade tree, suntan lotion, awning, sun umbrella, parasol, sunbonnet, hat, visor|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(16) What words are used of telling time by the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sundial, angle of the sun, sun-clock, shoot the sun, position of the sun,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(17) What words refer to using the power of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
solar energy, solar power, solar panel|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Moon|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Use this domain for words related to the moon. In your culture people may believe things about the moon. For instance in European culture people used to believe that the moon caused people to become crazy. So in English we have words like "moon-struck" and "lunatic." You should include such words in this domain.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

Use this domain for words related to planets (large objects that circle the sun, looking like bright wandering stars in the sky), comets (objects that circle the sun, looking like a star with a tail), meteors (small objects that come from space and burn up when they hit the earth's atmosphere, causing a streak of light across the sky), and asteroids (small objects that circle the sun), planetary moons (large objects that circle the planets). Some cultures do not study the stars and will have few or no words in this domain. Others cultures that study the stars will have many words. There are only five planets that people can see in the sky--Mercury, Venus, Mars, Jupiter, and Saturn. The others are only known from the scientific study of astronomy.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(1) What words refer to a planet?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
planet, planetary, wandering star|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(2) What are the names of the planets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Mercury, Venus (Morning Star, Evening Star), Earth, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Uranus, Neptune, Pluto|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(3) What words refer to how the planets move?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
revolve (around the sun), orbit,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(4) What words refer to the sun and planets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
solar system|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

comet, tail, head|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(6) What do comets do?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
appear, point, fade|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

The others are only known from the scientific study of astronomy.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(1) What words refer to a planet?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
planet, planetary, wandering star|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(2) What are the names of the planets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Mercury, Venus (Morning Star, Evening Star), Earth, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Uranus, Neptune, Pluto|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(3) What words refer to how the planets move?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
revolve (around the sun), orbit,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(4) What words refer to the sun and planets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
solar system|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(5) What words refer to comets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
comet, tail, head|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(6) What do comets do?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
appear, point, fade|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(7) What words refer to meteors?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(2) What words refer to how the sun moves?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
rise, set, cross the sky, come up, go down, sink|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(3) What words refer to the time when the sun rises?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
dawn, sunrise, sunup, daybreak, cockcrow,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(4) What words refer to the time when the sun is at its highest point?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
noon, zenith,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(5) What words refer to the time when the sun sets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunset, dusk, sundown, twilight, eventide,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(6) What words refer to when the sun is shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
shine, sunny, bright, give light, be sunshiny, daytime,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(7) What words refer to the sun shining through the clouds?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
come out, break through (the clouds), go behind (a cloud)|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(8) What words describe where the sun is shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunlit, be (out) in the sun, lit by the sun, shine on, be in the sunlight, sunny (spot)|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(9) What words describe when or where the sun doesn't shine?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
shade, eclipse of the sun, sunless, shady, shadow, eclipse (v),|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(10) What words refer to the light of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunlight, ray, sunshine, beam, light, sunbeam, radiance, glow, sparkle, glisten, glare|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(11) What words describe the brightness of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
bright, intense, brilliant, blinding, glaring, glistening, luminous, dim|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(12) What refer to the sun heating things?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
warm, heat, dry|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(13) What else does the sun do?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
looks down on|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(14) What words describe the damage done by sunlight?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunburn, sunstroke, suntan, tan, heatstroke, heat prostration, sun damage, fading from the sun, bleached by the sun|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(15) What do people use to protect themselves from the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunglasses, shade tree, suntan lotion, awning, sun umbrella, parasol, sunbonnet, hat, visor|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(16) What words are used of telling time by the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sundial, angle of the sun, sun-clock, shoot the sun, position of the sun,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(17) What words refer to using the power of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
solar energy, solar power, solar panel|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Moon|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Use this domain for words related to the moon. In your culture people may believe things about the moon. For instance in European culture people used to believe that the moon caused people to become crazy. So in English we have words like "moon-struck" and "lunatic." You should include such words in this domain.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(1) What words refer to the moon?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
moon, lunar, satellite|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

rise, set, sink|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(3) What words refer to the time when the moon rises?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
moonrise, rising of the moon,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(4) What words refer to the time when the moon sets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
moonset, setting of the moon,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(5) What words refer to when the moon is shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
moon is shining, by the light of the moon, moon is/comes out,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(6) What words describe where the moon is shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
moonlit, be in the moonlight, lit by the moon, shine on,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(7) What words describe when or where the moon doesn't shine?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
moonless night, eclipse of the moon, eclipse (v),|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(8) What words refer to the light of the moon?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
moonlight, moonbeam, moonshine,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(9) What words describe the brightness of the moon?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
bright, pale,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(10) What words describe the appearance of the moon?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
man in the moon, harvest moon|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(11) What words refer to the spots on the moon?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
lunar sea, crater,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(12) What words refer to the phases of the moon?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
phase, new moon, full moon, half moon, quarter moon, crescent, sliver, moon is waxing (getting bigger), moon is waning (getting smaller), wax and wane|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(13) What words refer to the time it takes for the moon to go through its phases?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(lunar) month|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Star|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Use this domain for words related to the stars and other heavenly bodies.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(1) What words are used to refer to the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
star, starry, stellar|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(2) What words describe the sky when the stars are shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
starlit (sky), (sky is) ablaze with stars, starry (sky), star studded (sky), stars are shining|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(3) What words are used for where the stars are shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
starlit, lit by the stars|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(4) What words are used for when or where the stars don't shine?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
starless (sky, night)|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(5) What words refer to the light of the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
starlight|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(6) What words describe the brightness of the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
bright, brilliant, dim, luminous|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(7) What words describe the appearance of the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
twinkle, wink, glittering, star shaped|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(8) What words refer to the study of the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
astronomy, astronomer, astrology, astrologer, stargazer, magi|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(9) What is a group of stars called?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
constellation, galaxy, nebula|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Planet|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Use this domain for words related to planets (large objects that circle the sun, looking like bright wandering stars in the sky), comets (objects that circle the sun, looking like a star with a tail), meteors (small objects that come from space and burn up when they hit the earth's atmosphere, causing a streak of light across the sky), and asteroids (small objects that circle the sun), planetary moons (large objects that circle the planets). Some cultures do not study the stars and will have few or no words in this domain. Others cultures that study the stars will have many words. There are only five planets that people can see in the sky--Mercury, Venus, Mars, Jupiter, and Saturn. The others are only known from the scientific study of astronomy.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

(8) What words describe where the sun is shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunlit, be (out) in the sun, lit by the sun, shine on, be in the sunlight, sunny (spot)|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(9) What words describe when or where the sun doesn't shine?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
shade, eclipse of the sun, sunless, shady, shadow, eclipse (v),|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(10) What words refer to the light of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunlight, ray, sunshine, beam, light, sunbeam, radiance, glow, sparkle, glisten, glare|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(11) What words describe the brightness of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
bright, intense, brilliant, blinding, glaring, glistening, luminous, dim|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(12) What refer to the sun heating things?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
warm, heat, dry|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(13) What else does the sun do?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
looks down on|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(14) What words describe the damage done by sunlight?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunburn, sunstroke, suntan, tan, heatstroke, heat prostration, sun damage, fading from the sun, bleached by the sun|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(15) What do people use to protect themselves from the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sunglasses, shade tree, suntan lotion, awning, sun umbrella, parasol, sunbonnet, hat, visor|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(16) What words are used of telling time by the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
sundial, angle of the sun, sun-clock, shoot the sun, position of the sun,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(17) What words refer to using the power of the sun?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
solar energy, solar power, solar panel|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Moon|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Use this domain for words related to the moon. In your culture people may believe things about the moon. For instance in European culture people used to believe that the moon caused people to become crazy. So in English we have words like "moon-struck" and "lunatic." You should include such words in this domain.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(1) What words refer to the moon?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
moon, lunar, satellite|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

moon is shining, by the light of the moon, moon is/comes out,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

moonlight, moonbeam, moonshine,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

(lunar) month|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

Use this domain for words related to the stars and other heavenly bodies.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

star, starry, stellar|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

starlit (sky), (sky is) ablaze with stars, starry (sky), star studded (sky), stars are shining|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(3) What words are used for where the stars are shining?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
starlit, lit by the stars|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(4) What words are used for when or where the stars don't shine?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
starless (sky, night)|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(5) What words refer to the light of the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
starlight|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(6) What words describe the brightness of the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
bright, brilliant, dim, luminous|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(7) What words describe the appearance of the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
twinkle, wink, glittering, star shaped|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(8) What words refer to the study of the stars?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
astronomy, astronomer, astrology, astrologer, stargazer, magi|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(9) What is a group of stars called?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
constellation, galaxy, nebula|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Planet|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Use this domain for words related to planets (large objects that circle the sun, looking like bright wandering stars in the sky), comets (objects that circle the sun, looking like a star with a tail), meteors (small objects that come from space and burn up when they hit the earth's atmosphere, causing a streak of light across the sky), and asteroids (small objects that circle the sun), planetary moons (large objects that circle the planets). Some cultures do not study the stars and will have few or no words in this domain. Others cultures that study the stars will have many words. There are only five planets that people can see in the sky--Mercury, Venus, Mars, Jupiter, and Saturn. The others are only known from the scientific study of astronomy.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(1) What words refer to a planet?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
planet, planetary, wandering star|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(2) What are the names of the planets?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Mercury, Venus (Morning Star, Evening Star), Earth, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Uranus, Neptune, Pluto|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(3) What words refer to how the planets move?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
revolve (around the sun), orbit,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

Planet|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
Use this domain for words related to planets (large objects that circle the sun, looking like bright wandering stars in the sky), comets (objects that circle the sun, looking like a star with a tail), meteors (small objects that come from space and burn up when they hit the earth's atmosphere, causing a streak of light across the sky), and asteroids (small objects that circle the sun), planetary moons (large objects that circle the planets). Some cultures do not study the stars and will have few or no words in this domain. Others cultures that study the stars will have many words. There are only five planets that people can see in the sky--Mercury, Venus, Mars, Jupiter, and Saturn. The others are only known from the scientific study of astronomy.|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
(1) What words refer to a planet?|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?
planet, planetary, wandering star|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

Mercury, Venus (Morning Star, Evening Star), Earth, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Uranus, Neptune, Pluto|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

revolve (around the sun), orbit,|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

solar system|(2) Watter woorde verwys na hoe die son beweeg?

humid, humidity, damp, dry, sticky, muggy|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(3) What words describe good air (such as when the air in a room is clean or doesn't smell bad)?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
fresh air, airy, well ventilated|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete

air out, ventilate|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete

weather, weather conditions, atmospheric (conditions)|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete

sunny, sunshine, clear (weather), good (weather), fair (weather), fine (day)|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(3) What words describe the weather when it is getting better?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
clear, clear up, sun comes out,|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(4) What words describe the weather when it is bad?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
bad, terrible, foul, inclement, rough, dirty sky, severe|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(5) What words describe the weather when it is getting worse?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
cloud up, deteriorate|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(6) What words describe the weather when it changes?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(cold/warm/storm) front|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(7) What words describe the weather when it stays the same?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
stretch (of good weather), keep up|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(8) What words are used to describe any kind of weather?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
rain or shine, all weather, in all weathers|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(9) What words describe the temperature?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
temperature, hot, warm, heat, cold, chilly, crisp, mild, unseasonably warm/cold, scorching, heat wave, cold spell, cold snap, frigid, freezing, be a chill in the air,|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(10) What words describe the weather when there is a lot of water in the air?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
humid, humidity, damp, sultry|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(11) What words refer to the type of weather a place normally has?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
climate, dry/wet/cold/hot climate, tropical, temperate|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete

weather, weather conditions, atmospheric (conditions)|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete

sunny, sunshine, clear (weather), good (weather), fair (weather), fine (day)|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(3) What words describe the weather when it is getting better?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
clear, clear up, sun comes out,|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(4) What words describe the weather when it is bad?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
bad, terrible, foul, inclement, rough, dirty sky, severe|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(5) What words describe the weather when it is getting worse?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
cloud up, deteriorate|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(6) What words describe the weather when it changes?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(cold/warm/storm) front|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(7) What words describe the weather when it stays the same?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
stretch (of good weather), keep up|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(8) What words are used to describe any kind of weather?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
rain or shine, all weather, in all weathers|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(9) What words describe the temperature?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
temperature, hot, warm, heat, cold, chilly, crisp, mild, unseasonably warm/cold, scorching, heat wave, cold spell, cold snap, frigid, freezing, be a chill in the air,|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(10) What words describe the weather when there is a lot of water in the air?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
humid, humidity, damp, sultry|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
(11) What words refer to the type of weather a place normally has?|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
climate, dry/wet/cold/hot climate, tropical, temperate|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete

thermometer, barometer, weathervane|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete

weather forecast, weather report, the weather, the outlook|meteoriet, skiet sterre, val ster meteoriet roete, meteoriete
